  в”ң рҹ”’ _attrs                   = Object{1}  L133726: for(var o in t._attrs) вҖ” keyed by hero index, each has _items with calculated attrs
  в”ң рҹ”’ _baseAttrs               = Object{1}  L133731: t._baseAttrs[o] вҖ” keyed by hero index, each has _items with base attrs (before talent)
  в”” рҹ”’ POWER (attr 21)          = calculated per hero  L133821: 21==p._id вҶ’ heroBaseAttr.power = floor(num)
  вң… CRITICAL AUDIT: 3/3 PASSED

  вҡ пёҸ  [WARN-001] chat-server must be running on http://127.0.0.1:8002
       Expected: (server operational)
       Got:      may fail if chat-server down
       Impact:   Chat will never connect. Client stops retrying registChat after 15 attempts (45s).
       Fix:      Ensure chat-server is started before main-server

  вҡ пёҸ  [WARN-002] chat-server MUST implement TEA handshake (verifyEnable=true)
       Expected: (TEA verify event emitted by chat-server)
       Got:      L113445: chatClient verifyEnable=TRUE вҶ’ waits for verify event
       Impact:   Client connection stalls вҖ” callback never fires, no chat, no error shown.
       Fix:      chat-server must emit "verify" event with TEA challenge on connect

  вҡ пёҸ  [WARN-003] guildRoomId, teamDungeonChatRoom, teamChatRoom = undefined (by design)
       Expected: (undefined for new/no-guild/no-team users)
       Got:      Returning undefined вҖ” client L114568/114579/114590 checks truthy before join
       Impact:   None вҖ” client correctly skips joining these rooms when undefined.
       Fix:      N/A вҖ” this is correct behavior. Guild handler (L114204) updates guildRoomId dynamically.

  в”ң рҹ”’ _changeInfo._items       = 5 items  L97686: getBattleAwardItems iterates _changeInfo._items for {_id, _num}
  в”ң рҹ”’ _curLess                 = 10102  L104892/L97751: OnHookSingleton.lastSection = e._curLess
  в”” рҹ”’ _maxPassLesson           = 10101  L104893/L97751: OnHookSingleton.maxPassLesson = e._maxPassLesson
  вң… CRITICAL AUDIT: 4/4 PASSED

  рҹ”’ CRITICAL FIELDS AUDIT вҖ” game will crash/stuck if wrong
  в”ң рҹ”’ _attrs                   = Object{1}  L133726: for(var o in t._attrs) вҖ” keyed by hero index, each has _items with calculated attrs
  в”ң рҹ”’ _baseAttrs               = Object{1}  L133731: t._baseAttrs[o] вҖ” keyed by hero index, each has _items with base attrs (before talent)
  в”” рҹ”’ POWER (attr 21)          = calculated per hero  L133821: 21==p._id вҶ’ heroBaseAttr.power = floor(num)
  вң… CRITICAL AUDIT: 3/3 PASSED

  рҹ”’ CRITICAL FIELDS AUDIT вҖ” game will crash/stuck if wrong
  в”ң рҹ”’ _attrs                   = Object{1}  L133726: for(var o in t._attrs) вҖ” keyed by hero index, each has _items with calculated attrs
  в”ң рҹ”’ _baseAttrs               = Object{1}  L133731: t._baseAttrs[o] вҖ” keyed by hero index, each has _items with base attrs (before talent)
  в”” рҹ”’ POWER (attr 21)          = calculated per hero  L133821: 21==p._id вҶ’ heroBaseAttr.power = floor(num)
  вң… CRITICAL AUDIT: 3/3 PASSED
